Central Political Conference

Two Hundred and Twenty-Second Meeting

The Central Political Conference held its two hundred and twenty-second political meeting at 8:00 am this morning (9th). Attendees included Wang Chonghui,

Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, Sun Ke, Chen Guofu, and Hu Hanmin.

Attendees included Li Wenfan, Chen Lifu, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Zhengting,

Liu Jiwen, and Fang Juehui. The chairman was Tan Yankai. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) A letter from the Central Executive Committee stated that the Central Training Department had submitted a draft of the principles of the Farmers' Association organization and the provisional regulations of the Farmers' Association for public decision. The case was handed over to the three departments of Organization, Propaganda, and Training, together with the Central Legal Regulations Compilation and Review Committee for review. Subsequently, the joint review and amendment of the principles of the Farmers' Association organization were presented, stating that after approval, the provisional regulations of the Farmers' Association will be reviewed based on the principles. The 83rd Standing Committee of this conference discussed the matter and decided to submit it to the Political Conference because it concerned the principles of legislation. The principles were specially sent for review. It was resolved to hand it over to the Political Report Group and the Economic Group for review. (2) A letter from the Central Executive Committee was opened, and a film censorship ordinance drafted by the Central Propaganda Department was submitted to the Political Conference by the 82nd Standing Committee of this conference and handed over to the Legislative Yuan for drafting into law according to the following principles: (1) Film censorship matters shall be handled by the special municipal governments, but the special municipal party departments shall send personnel to participate in the guidance. (2) After censorship in location A,

Location B is exempt from censorship. (3) Censorship procedures should be simplified and expedited. (4) Domestic films are exempt from censorship fees. Please check and handle. It was resolved to hand it over to the Legislative Yuan. (3) The Central Executive Committee transferred a telegram from the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee, approving the Hunan Provincial County Magistrate Qualification Review Committee's request for an interpretation of whether party affairs work can

be considered administrative affairs, and requested instructions to comply with. It was resolved to hand it over to the Political Report Group for review.

Soviet Party Rectification Conference

Please Protest Japanese Warships Sailing to China

The Jiangsu Provincial Party Rectification Committee recently submitted a request to the Central Party Headquarters to seriously protest the sailing of Japanese warships to China. The submitted document is recorded as follows: "According to reports,

fifteen destroyers of the Japanese First Hydroelectric Squadron suddenly departed from the Sasebo Naval Port in that country to China, ostensibly to practice navigation routes. They went straight into various key ports of the Yangtze River in our country. When the news came, everyone was shocked and horrified. It is found that independent countries in the world not only do not allow others to invade their domestic navigation rights, but also do not allow others to intervene in their territorial waters. Since the Opium War, our country has been

bound by unequal treaties, and foreign merchant ships have been able to freely enter and exit inland rivers, encroaching on sovereignty and manipulating commerce. The economic losses suffered by our people are incalculable.

Now, Japanese imperialists are intensifying their efforts and directly regard our country as a non-independent country. They dare to order their large fleet, fully loaded with soldiers, to sail into the hinterland of our country. Only the Japanese naval attaché orally notified our naval department and the Beijing Municipal Government.

This is an unprecedented example in the international community, insulting our country and encroaching on our sovereignty. It is truly intolerable. Party departments and people at all levels in this province are all heartbroken and indignant, and are calling for action. They should ask the headquarters to protest sternly in order to calm public anger. As for the excuse of practicing navigation routes, the Yangtze River is our country's inland river. It is not comparable to the Rhine River in Germany today, which is managed by the powers. If the Japanese fleet wants to practice navigation, the vast Pacific Ocean is vast and unobstructed, and they can practice freely. Why must they take our country's Yangtze River as their destination for practice? It can be imagined that they are spying on our national defense and intending to create an excuse to start

a war. Recalling that when our party sent troops to the Northern Expedition, Japan took the violent action of sending troops to Shandong. Last year, Feng Yuxiang rebelled,

and there was an internal invasion by Red Russia. From the past, every time there was a disturbance in the country, there were imperialists who were secretly planning it. This time, the rebels Yan Xishan and others were in arms to create turmoil, and the Japanese destroyer fleet happened to come to China in a big way at this time. A glimpse of their intentions is infuriating. The members of the association feel the blood of the May 3rd tragedy has not yet dried, and they have witnessed the rampantness of Japanese warships. They are worried and disturbed, and it is difficult to remain silent. I respectfully express my stupid sincerity and humbly pray for your consideration. I am eagerly looking forward to it."

Status of Nanchang-Xunyang Railway After Being Handled by the Ministry

Operating Income Increases Year by Year

The Bureau Plans to Expand

Nanchang Communication, 8th - The Nanchang-Xunyang Railway is the throat of Jiangxi transportation. The entire line is more than 300 li long, with 10 locomotives and more than 100 passenger and freight cars. The Japanese debt it owes amounts to more than 10 million Japanese yen, and the situation is precarious and bankruptcy is imminent. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways took over the railway in January of the 18th year and appointed Long Xuesui as the director of the railway bureau to engage in rectification. When the railway was taken over by the Ministry, the monthly income was only more than 95,000 yuan, reaching more than 130,000 yuan in April, and averaging more than 120,000 yuan per month thereafter. Therefore, the income for the 18th year was quite considerable, with 749,500 yuan in passenger business, 696,700 yuan in freight business, and more than 12,500 yuan in other businesses, totaling more than 1,458,700 yuan. After deducting expenses, there was a surplus of more than 240,000 yuan, which was unprecedented (previously, expenses exceeded income). Yesterday,

I met with a certain staff member of the accounting department of the railway, who said that the operating income of the railway increased by more than 130,000 yuan in the 16th year compared with the 15th year,

increased by more than 230,000 yuan in the 17th year compared with the 16th year, and increased by more than 290,000 yuan in the 18th year compared with the 17th year.

If there were no rice exports this year, it could have increased by more than 300,000 yuan. It is heard that Director Long, in addition to personally crossing the East China Sea a few days ago to earnestly discuss with the creditor, the Japanese East Asia Industrial Co., Ltd., to reduce interest and schedule annual amortization, has also formulated the 19th-year expansion plan: (1) In terms of general affairs, strengthen the road protection team,

to prevent bandits and ensure the safety of traffic. (2) In terms of engineering, A. decide to revise the uneven parts of the road and those with too small a curvature to facilitate traffic and avoid danger; B. install water pipes and build water towers at the three stations of Nanchang Tujiapu and Dean; C.

rebuild the buildings of each station; D. clean up the land; E.

plant seedlings by the roadside to cultivate sleeper materials. (3) In terms of car operations, A. set up a pontoon boat on each bank of the Nanchang Zhangjiangmen ferry to facilitate communication; B. recruit merchants to open restaurants at the Niuxing Station to facilitate travelers. (4) In terms of machinery, A.

increase 2 locomotives, 8 passenger cars, and 40 freight cars;

B. build a new machine factory and purchase a 200-kilowatt generator to tow all the machines in the factory so that all types of locomotives can be repaired on schedule.

Nanyang Minxin Bureau Cancelled

Re-establishment of Postal Agency

Singapore and Xiamen postal agencies still oppose Xiamen communications. Many overseas Chinese from Southern Fujian and Chaozhou-Meixian who reside in Nanyang establish postal agencies to send letters and remittances for overseas Chinese. Initially, they sent it themselves, but after the ban by the British, Dutch, French, American governments in Nanyang and our country's post office,

they changed to general mail packing, that is, a number of letters are sent as a general package,

After arrival, the postal agency distributes them by themselves. However, this still does not comply with the Universal Postal Convention. After mutual consultation between our country and the Nanyang government, each postal agency is allowed to be changed to a special postal agency. However, each letter sent must have sufficient postage affixed. Last November, Lin Zhuowu, special commissioner of postal affairs of the Ministry of Communications, came to Xiamen to consult with various postal agencies in Xiamen. As a result, they agreed to postpone the implementation for four months. The British Nanyang Chinese Postal Agency also asked the local government to allow a four-month postponement. April 1 of this year is the date when our country and British Nanyang will implement it simultaneously. The Xiamen Post Office issued the regulations for special postal agencies on the 1st. The original text is as follows:

Article 1: The Post Office establishes special postal agencies to unify the postal service and facilitate overseas Chinese communication. They are reorganized from private postal agencies that have been licensed for overseas business.

Article 2: When a private postal agency that has been licensed for overseas business is reorganized into a special postal agency, it shall first submit the original license for verification, fill out a petition in the format prepared by the Post Office, and request the competent Post Office to forward it to the Directorate General of Posts for approval and registration, and exchange it for a special postal agency license as a business certificate. If the aforementioned license is damaged or lost, the reason may be stated and a request for re-issuance may be made. However, the license shall not be transferred to others.

Article 3: Any private postal agency requesting reorganization into a special postal agency,

If there are branch offices that have been registered, they shall be clearly stated in the petition. After being approved and registered by the Directorate General of Posts, they may be reorganized into special postal agency branch offices, and the name and location of the branch office shall be recorded in the special postal agency license for reference.

Article 4: Each special postal agency and its branch offices shall be subject to the jurisdiction and supervision of the local post office and shall comply with all post office regulations.

Article 5: Special postal agencies are only allowed to receive and send return letters of foreign remittances, ordinary letters, and postcards. Each item shall be charged according to the national international postage rates.

Article 6: Special postal agencies shall comply with the postal regulations, affix international postage to each letter (i.e., return letter) sent abroad, and hand it over to the post office for delivery. Each envelope shall contain only one letter and shall not contain letters with different names from those written on the envelope. However, for the sake of convenience, they are allowed to be bundled and submitted to the post office for dispatch.

Article 7: When a special postal agency receives letters from abroad that have sufficient international postage affixed according to international rates, when forwarding them to the interior,

domestic postage is waived. Letters sent from the interior to foreign countries that need to be transferred through the exchange office are also allowed to affix sufficient international postage in the interior first, and there is no need to pay domestic postage again.

Article 8: The validity period of the license of a special postal agency is one year and shall be renewed every year. Each time, a handling fee of one yuan in national currency shall be paid per license. Each special postal agency shall submit a petition to the competent post office before December 1 of each year to forward it to the Directorate General of Posts for a new license. When issuing a new license, the Directorate General of Posts shall issue a license renewal permit to notify each special agency.

The old license shall be submitted to the competent post office for cancellation and a new license shall be obtained. Those who request re-issuance of a license in accordance with the provisions of Article 2, Paragraph 3 shall also pay a handling fee of one yuan in national currency.

Article 9: When a private postal agency requesting reorganization into a special postal agency is approved by the Directorate General of Posts and a license is issued, the competent post office shall also issue a signboard with the words "Special Postal Agency", charging two yuan in national currency for each. The same applies to special postal agency branch offices.

Article 10: Any private postal agency that has been licensed for overseas business, if it wishes to be reorganized into a special postal agency, shall submit the original license of the private postal agency to the post office within one month after the implementation of these regulations to request approval for registration and exchange for a special postal agency license. If the deadline is exceeded, it will not be issued and the original license of the private postal agency will be canceled.

Article 11: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

The Ministry of Communications also sent Lin Zhuowu to Xiamen and Zhou Yundong to Shantou,

to explain to the private postal agencies. However, on the 2nd of this month, the local Postal Industry Association suddenly received a telegram from the Nanyang British Singapore Overseas Chinese Assembly,

saying, "Here, the reduction is six cents per letter, and the general package remains the same. It is implemented today. We have telegraphed the Ministry to request approval to keep it as it is, at most doubling it from before," and so on. On the 3rd, more than 70 representatives of the postal industry consulted with Lin Zhuowu to postpone the exchange of licenses and submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications to reduce postage and retain the private postal agency and general package system. Important News 2

Reply from the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department

Reorganization of Suzhou Municipal Organs

The Jiangsu Provincial Government, regarding the reorganization of the Suzhou municipal organs,

Previously, it was resolved by the 275th Committee Meeting and handed over to the Department of Civil Affairs for review. Now, Director Hu has prepared a document to reply. The original text is recorded as follows: "According to the instructions in Order No. 1369 of your government, according to the resolution of the 275th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, the Suzhou Municipal Government will be abolished in principle, administrative expenses will be reduced, and business expenses will be expanded. As for the takeover of organs and the continuation of business, it will be handed over to the Department of Civil Affairs for review, etc. Upon receiving this, I hereby record the case and order the department to comply and handle it, etc. I secretly investigated the takeover file,

Since Suzhou presented the establishment of the city, its municipal government's administrative expenses in the 17th year of the Republic accounted for almost one-third of the city's business expenses, which is very different from the principle that the city's administrative expenses account for one-fifth of the business expenses. Although repeated orders have been issued to tighten up, there has been no sincere compliance. Therefore, the progress of emerging construction is slow, and the infusion of existing business expenses is difficult. Daily discussions of digging and scraping are causing citizens to blame each other. All of this is due to the fact that the original organizational scope is not compatible with the economic reality of the city. Changing the course is already urgent. Recently, the Legislative Yuan, in view of the fact that the spirit of the past municipal system did not conform to local realities, has set another principle draft and is engaged in revision. The conditions for setting up a Class B city in Article 4 (

1) The population is over 300,000; (2) There are special circumstances in politics, economics, or national defense; (3) Business tax. The annual income of license fees and land tax accounts for one-half of the city's total fiscal revenue. Now, according to Suzhou's population, it is only 260,000 or so. The provincial capital of the Republic of China was moved,

There are few special circumstances in politics, economics, and national defense.

Business and land taxes have not yet been opened, and license fees are not under the jurisdiction of the city. Therefore, Suzhou City has lost the conditions for a Class B city under the new principles. The decision of the Committee Meeting of Your Government to abolish the municipal government of the city in principle is indeed very appropriate, but

The municipal government of Suzhou should be abolished, but the municipal administration of Suzhou should not be interrupted for a day. According to the draft municipal organization principles, in addition to Class A and Class B cities, there are provisions for Class C cities. Class C cities establish municipal offices, under which there are bureaus or sections. The mayor is recommended or appointed, and a municipal council is set up in the municipal office. This principle,

It is most suitable for the orders of your government. The Department of Civil Affairs intends to directly change the establishment of Suzhou Municipal Office in Suzhou, take over the original municipal government organs, simplify the organization as much as possible, reduce administrative expenses as much as possible,

Expand business expenses and continue to handle it. In terms of the status of Suzhou City, the mayor's treatment is proposed to be recommended and still belongs to the provincial government, with the Department of Civil Affairs as the competent authority. As for the internal organization of the municipal office, after this case is approved, the Department of Civil Affairs will formulate and submit it for approval in another case."

Recent Financial Situation of Guangdong and Guangxi Provinces

Guangdong's military expenditure requires 4.5 million per month. Guangxi Province has no tax revenue and paper money is scarce.

Guangzhou correspondence. Guangdong Province has recently used troops in Guangxi Province. It is reported that the military expenditure in March has increased to 4.5 million yuan. As of the 31st, 3.8 million yuan of military expenditure last month has been spent. On the 3rd of this month, the Department of Finance allocated another 350,000 yuan in cash.

Escorted to Wuzhou and handed over to the Eighth Route Army for distribution. It is found that 350,000 yuan of military expenditure in March is still owed. As for the expenses of various agencies in February, they were delayed until the beginning of this month and have not yet been cleared. It is estimated that the administrative expenses in February will be cleared in mid-month. The treasury bonds for military needs issued by the Department of Finance some time ago have recently sold 2.54 million yuan, and there are still 1.46 million yuan left, which are currently being promoted. It is expected that they will be sold out in a month. In addition, the Tariff Committee recently decided to hold eight special taxes to increase revenue. It is found that in July last year, the committee decided to completely cut off the Likin tax in the province in February this year. At the same time, special consumption taxes such as timber, livestock, paper, minerals, soybeans, cotton, fur, and tin foil were held. On the 1st of this month, the committee held the 39th meeting and immediately decided to hold it. The next meeting will discuss the investigation methods. After the investigation is clear, the tax rate will be discussed and the collection regulations will be drafted. In the future, when the tax is levied,

the government's estimated income will be enough to offset the Likin tax that has been cut off. As for the financial situation of Guangxi Province, since the outbreak of the civil war in the province,

the financial situation has fallen into a stalemate. In the past, Wuzhou was the concentration of wealth in Guangxi, and the interior areas were all barren areas. For the past two years, the war has been endless, and local finances are equal to the farmers looking up at the roof.

Business is declining, and the source of income is naturally cut off. The so-called relatively wealthy Wuzhou is still within the scope of military affairs. The loss of Guangxi banknotes suffered by the people of Wuzhou is particularly painful.

The Guangxi banknotes were issued by the Guangxi government in the past few years, almost tens of millions. After Huang Shaoxiong and others failed, the government collapsed, and the Guangxi banknotes were not guaranteed. At first, it fell to 30%, and now it has become waste

paper. Currently, the Wuzhou General Chamber of Commerce has sealed up more than 3.2 million Guangxi banknotes. The Wuzhou merchants and the people of Guangxi have suffered huge losses, and the business of Wuzhou City has plummeted, and countless people have gone bankrupt. Recently, Liang Elian, the Director of the Wuzhou Finance Office appointed by the Central Government, has formulated a method to maintain the waste currency and is implementing it with discretion. However, it is found that in Nanning and Liuzhou, Li Huang

and others are still wantonly issuing this paper money, which is difficult to guarantee not to be mixed into Wuzhou. If so, the maintenance here and the wanton issuance there will inevitably have zero effect. Therefore, recently, in order to prevent the paper money wantonly issued by the other party from being mixed into Wuzhou City, the Finance Office has specially notified the people of Wuzhou City to take the paper money they had previously stored to the Chamber of Commerce for registration and transfer for safekeeping in order to start trying to maintain it. (April 4th)

Establishment of Financial Consolidation Committee in Northeast China

Shenyang correspondence. In recent years, the currency law in Northeast China has been scarce, the people are poor and the wealth is difficult, the number of foreign currencies is increasing day by day, the local currency is becoming more and more chaotic, the provincial finances are in deficit, the financial sector is extremely tight, and all industries are declining.

The dangerous situation is fully revealed. If a thorough solution is not studied as soon as possible, in two or three years, the treasury will be empty and the people will be poor. Not only will the finances of the entire province be in danger of bankruptcy, but tens of millions of people in the eastern province will also sigh. Currently, Ning Encheng, the chief auditor of the Border Industry Bank, has suggested establishing the Financial Consolidation Committee of the Three Eastern Provinces, and the government has hired five or six financial experts, banking tycoons, and specialized talents in the industry to study consolidation methods and seek fundamental remedies. After being forwarded by the Liaoning Provincial Government to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for approval,

Five people, including Ning Encheng, Jing You, Xiao Chunmou, and Lin Chengxiu, have been hired as members, and the organization will be established soon. The organization regulations of the committee are recorded as follows: (1) Name: This committee is named the Financial Consolidation Committee of the Three Eastern Provinces. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this committee is to study the consolidation policies of the financial sector of the Three Eastern Provinces and to discuss the design of finance. (3) Organization: A. This committee has five members, two secretaries, two stenographers, and two clerks. The members are selected by the Northeast Political Affairs Committee from five financial experts and specialized talents in the industry. B. This committee has several consultants. C. Before the official establishment of this committee, the Liaoning Provincial Government may establish the Liaoning Provincial Financial Consolidation Committee. The time limit for its establishment shall be until the date of establishment of this committee.

D. Except for the secretary, stenographer, and clerk, the members and consultants of this committee,

are not paid salaries. (4) Duties: A. This committee shall, based on the research results and the discussion policies, prepare a report and submit it to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee in the shortest possible time to request its adoption and implementation. B. The report of this committee can be divided into two parts: preliminary and formal. The preliminary report only describes the palliative measures,

As for the fundamental solution, it will be detailed in the formal report. C. This committee has the responsibility to present opinions to any financial institution. (5) Authority: A. This committee may requisition any secret and non-secret cases, account books, tables, charts, and descriptions from financial and financial institutions, but when necessary, it shall strictly keep certain cases confidential. B. This committee may invite any person to attend the meeting to express opinions. (6) Meetings: Except for Saturdays and Sundays, this committee shall hold meetings every day from 11:00 am to 3:00 pm. (7) Expenses:

The expenses of this committee shall be reimbursed for actual expenses, but shall not exceed 1,000 yuan in national currency per month, and shall be submitted to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for approval and payment. (8) Address: (9) Term: This committee shall be dissolved immediately after the formal report is submitted to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee.

(April 2nd)

Harbin Strictly Prevents Communist Propaganda

Inspect Mail and Telegraph, Investigate Household Registration

And Set Fundamental Prevention Plan

Harbin correspondence. In the past month, the Third International has been trying its best to promote propaganda in Harbin. Chinese youth who are willing to be raised by others and driven to do the most effective redification work, such as the Anti-Imperialist League, the People's Mutual Aid Association, etc., have been established one after another, and leaflets containing incitement to strikes and school strikes have been distributed. The authorities are afraid of affecting the overall situation and have repeatedly tolerated it, resulting in the Communist Party's activities being openly unscrupulous. Recently, the Northeast Political Committee received a report, sincerely fearing that Harbin City would suffer from communism

bloodshed, especially yesterday ordered the Special Zone Chief Executive Office,

to forward the order to all subordinates to prevent it together, and to implement inspection of mail and telegraph, and investigation of household registration. The order is recorded as follows: "According to reports, the Communist Party in Harbin is distributing leaflets, openly opposing the party and the country, and supporting the Soviet Union. Mad teachers and journalists are in contact with party members, specializing in inciting students and mobilizing workers. First, they want to use railway workers, and then they want to lure local workers. Although the police have repeatedly cracked down, the crackdown is a crackdown, and the progress is its own progress. The distributed leaflets are signed by the Harbin Youth Anti-Imperialist League, claiming to be the Harbin Municipal Committee of the Communist Party of China, and are sent by the post office in vernacular newspapers. After translating the meaning of each single report, it is purely the tone of the Soviet Union, propagating redification,

If we allow it to continue and do not take precautions, Harbin will soon become the Third International. For the sake of the security of the Northeast, for the sake of the East

For the sake of consolidating the road, there must be a fundamental plan for the administration of Harbin. First, party affairs must be handled slowly, and party newspapers must also be set up slowly,

to avoid excessive promotion and flowing into communist propaganda. Second, schools must be strictly rectified. On the one hand, bad teachers should be eliminated, and on the other hand, bad students should be screened. Do not tolerate perfunctorily and nurture disaster-causing elements. Third, railway workers must be managed by us with extremely strict and appropriate methods, so that workers' rights

can be guaranteed, and prevent and stop at any time, to avoid being infected by foreigners.

In addition, for the inspection of mail and the investigation of household registration, the police should seriously carry out the work, or they may be able to eliminate the disaster invisibly, etc. In view of this, in addition to separate orders, the said office is ordered to formulate practical methods within its respective duties, strictly prevent it, and supervise and order its subordinates to prevent it separately, so as not to spread it, and to report the implementation situation for reply, etc. In view of this, the party factions in Harbin are complex,

Workers and students are mixed, and personnel have been sent to investigate at any time. Then, according to the secret report from the said place, we have already taken separate actions to prevent it. Now, in view of the foregoing, as for the sections on slowing down the handling of party newspapers, inspecting mail and telegraph, and investigating household registration opened in the original order, which belong to the duties of the said office, they should immediately comply with the order and seriously handle them, and supervise and order their subordinates,

Investigate and prevent at any time to maintain security, and report the handling situation for verification. "It is found that the Harbin Republic of China Daily Party Newspaper,

was originally scheduled to be published on April 1, but the authorities have the aforementioned order,

So the publication was suspended. (2nd)

Establishment of Diplomatic Commissioner's Office in Harbin

Zhong Yu Takes Office in Harbin

Harbin correspondence. Zhong Yu, Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Harbin, arrived in Harbin from Jilin on the afternoon of March 30. In the evening, he visited Mo Dehui, the director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and talked about the formalities for notifying the Russian side of the Sino-Russian meeting. At 10:00 am today, he formed the Commissioner's Office in the old Negotiation Office. At noon, he went to Daowai to take up the concurrent position of Director of the Binjiang Municipal Preparatory Office. Recently, I visited Mr. Zhong and asked when he would notify the Russian side of the date of Mo's plenipotentiary's departure and the date of convening the meeting. Zhong said that this matter was only decided when he met with Director Mo the night before. I will handle the notification. However, I have not yet sorted out the Sino-Russian negotiation files clearly. How to word the notification letter,

There are places that need to be considered, so when it will be delivered to the Russian Consulate is still undecided. Before the notification is issued, it is tentatively planned not to visit the Russian Consulate.

The reporter asked again whether he would go to Russia with Mo's plenipotentiary in the future. Zhong replied that the entourage of Mo's plenipotentiary, except for those designated by the central government, are all personnel from the Chinese Eastern Railway and have been confirmed. I have no need to go with them. When asked about the organization of the office, Zhong replied that in accordance with the orders issued by the central government, in addition to the special commissioner, there will be one director,

several secretaries and staff members. The departmental system is not adopted, and the detailed rules for handling affairs will be drafted by me and submitted to the central government for approval. A office is also set up in Jilin, and a director and several staff members are responsible.

Important matters should be reported at any time. Changchun and Yanji are still handled concurrently by the respective municipal preparatory offices, but they are of a entrusted nature and consult by letter at any time when things happen. In short, all foreign affairs in the province will be concentrated in Harbin from now on. The Commissioner's Office in Liaoning will take a departmental system due to different circumstances. As for Mo Dehui's luggage, it is being actively prepared. Li Chen, an external entourage member, arrived in Harbin on the evening of March 31. All entourage members are also rushing to prepare their luggage. Mo himself plans to go to France and Germany after the Moscow meeting and inspect the road administration along the way. (April 1st)

Hangzhou Decision Letter

The local construction meeting convened by the Construction Department was held at 1:00 pm today (9th) for the opening ceremony. Dai Jitao, Minister of Training of the Central Government, and Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Provincial Government, both attended the meeting to give instructions. Eighty-one representatives from various counties attended the meeting. After the meeting, the assembly elected reviewers and divided them into six groups to review the proposals. Tomorrow, the whole body will participate in the National Games, and the official meeting will begin on the 11th.

Zhejiang Province has been handling immigration and reclamation for a long time. The provincial government now has more than 1,300 disaster victims from Wenzhou, Taizhou, Ningbo, Shaoxing, Hangzhou and other places reporting. Yesterday, it telegraphed the Northeast authorities to first transfer 400 households, which will depart from Shanghai by boat on the 20th of this month and land at Yingkou. Because the people of Zhejiang are accustomed to planting rice, the telegram also asked them to be settled in rice-growing areas.

In the case of Haiyan Xucun Market's abolition of frying and changing to sun-drying, the Liangzhe Salt Transport Department has repeatedly received requests from various stove merchants and all frying workers in the market to gradually reduce the number of years in order to seek to change careers gradually, and the magistrate of the market has submitted a request to exempt the phased reduction and extend the period to the end of the 19th year, when all stoves will be stopped at the same time. The Salt Affairs Department has now approved the extension of the period to the end of December this year and implemented sun-drying. The order has been forwarded yesterday for compliance.

The price of rice in Hangzhou City has risen sharply, with top-quality rice at 16.2 yuan per stone and starting rice at 13.6 yuan. In the past two weeks, the source is still lacking, and the market has increased again. Rice merchants are deeply feeling the difficulty. This afternoon (9th), the Municipal and County Rice Price Council held the 55th regular meeting at the Municipal Government. It has been decided to increase the price of rice of the upper and middle grades by 40 cents, and the starting rice will remain at the original price. It was also discussed that before the opening of the plain rice in the city, the starting rice is related to the livelihood of the poor and will not be increased for the time being.

Jiang Erchang's Trial Record. Jiang Erchang, the former executive member of this county, was arrested and imprisoned privately for Zhang Youshu's book. After the victim's nephew, Fang Qin, told the county government, he secretly ordered Yin Risheng, the captain of the second team of the police, to lead the team to the countryside and bring Jiang Erchang and the victim, Zhang Youshu, etc., together with the seized guns, ammunition, and discarded national flags, to the county government for interrogation. Last night (8th), late at night, Du Cheng, the interrogator, opened the court for interrogation and ordered that no one be allowed to listen. Now, I know that Jiang Erchang's statement roughly said that Zhang Youshu's nephew, Fang Qin, abducted and seduced his sister to escape with her belongings. After arriving in Songjiang, he hired a boat at Malu Bridge to escape to Zhang Youshu's house in Qingyi County. When he heard the news and went to find him, he had already heard the news and left. He ordered Youshu to hand over the person, but Youshu refused to admit it and was willing to come to my house as a hostage to clarify the truth. As for the guns, ammunition, and bayonets used by the guard regiment, they all have passports and are not privately hidden. The old five-color national flag was made when he was studying in the past. After being discarded, it was used for wrapping

and stored in a box. The examiner then ordered that the case be investigated and temporarily detained for verification,

and prohibited visits during the investigation.

Fengxian

Collection of Land Transaction Commission, District Chief Joint Association: Due to the lack of funds for the former Zhenxiang Public Office, it was proposed to collect 20% of the land transaction commission to be used for offsetting expenses, which has been approved by the county government and a notice has been issued for compliance.

The method is that for all private land transaction deeds, 20% of the amount must be paid to the district, and a stamp indicating receipt must be affixed before tax payment is allowed. Those who fail to pay will be required to pay the difference during land registration. To clarify the boundaries, the collection date is set to begin on January 1, Year 19. All land deeds established in January that have not been taxed must also pay the difference. Instructions and notices have already been issued separately.

Confiscation of Property from Prostitution and Heretical Temples: Previously, each district was notified to investigate, fill out forms, and ban prostitution and heretical temples. All properties of those that should be abolished have also been resolved by the district offices to be confiscated and reallocated for Zhenxiang expenses. The county government has now submitted this to the province for approval, and a notice was specially issued yesterday, limiting the original managers to hand over the property deeds, income and expenses, and remaining funds to the district office for management within two weeks. Those who conceal or resist will be arrested and forced to hand over the items by the Public Security Bureau. It is said that the most such property is located along the eastern Tang area.

Jiading

Investigation of Road Dispute: There is an original road in Beishi of Anting Town, which is the only way for farmers in the northeast to go to the market. However, the land on both sides is owned by the Xiaoxing Church of the 教會. In the middle of last month, the church was constructing something and planned to build a bamboo fence, making it difficult for pedestrians to pass. The citizens tried to stop it without success, so they filed a public complaint with the county government requesting an order for its removal. After receiving the complaint, County Magistrate Chen sent Pan Zhixing, the section chief of the Second Section, to investigate the site yesterday (7th). It was confirmed that it has been a thoroughfare for many years. A map has been drawn and submitted with an accurate report.

Response to the Reorganization of the Provincial Education Fund Management Office: The County Education Bureau and the Education Association, in response to reports that the cities of Beijing and Shanghai are competing to collect slaughter tax funds, the three ministers of finance, education, and foreign affairs plan to reply to the National Government to reorganize the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office, adding the heads of the finance and education bureaus of Beijing and Shanghai as members, not canceling the independent funding of Jiangsu education, and transferring schools such as Shanghai Middle School to the management of the cities of Beijing and Shanghai. The expenses will still be paid by the management office, but the schools will be owned by the cities and the expenses will be the responsibility of Jiangsu, which will lead to inconsistent authority and many disputes. A telegram was sent to Chairman Chiang, President Tan, the Ministry of Education, the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and the Department of Education, requesting them to make every effort to reverse the decision and dismiss the previous proposal, and also requesting the educational circles of Jiangsu Province to strive together.

Wuxi

Actively Preparing to Suppress Lake Bandits: The Second District of the Provincial Public Security Water Police Team stationed in Wuxi, received a telegram from the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters, ordering the Zhaowu and Jinghu ships under its jurisdiction to be transferred to the direct command of the headquarters for deployment. Furthermore, the Jialu and Hongping ships, as well as the Sian patrol ship originally under the jurisdiction of the Third District of the Zhejiang Inland River Water Police Bureau, were transferred to the direct command of Zhong Yuanhang Yi, the commander of the Western District. You and others hid in Shanghai and recently returned to Wuxi to engage in activities. After questioning by Chief Ni, they confessed to joining the Communist Party and extorting large sums from villagers. However, they firmly denied major crimes such as murder, arson, and kidnapping for ransom. Chief Ni, based on the confession, prepared a document and sent it to the district office to await interrogation and handling.

Additional Notes on Kidnapping Cases: Around 10:00 p.m. on the 1st, over two hundred bandits suddenly came to the home of Zhang Ziyan, the richest man in the northwest township of Lifà, and broke in over the walls. The owner seized the opportunity to escape, but his four sons were captured by the bandits and severely beaten, with serious injuries to their lower bodies. After looting, they burned down thirty-one main houses, resulting in a loss of over twenty thousand gold coins. Furthermore, over twenty bandits armed with guns and flashlights suddenly came to the home of Ma Jianbo in Luzhuang Township, northwest of Rugao City, on the night of the 2nd and broke in. Ma was unable to escape and was kidnapped by the bandits. On the same day, multiple bandits also came to the home of the wealthy Tang Zimu in Lujiazhuang, armed with guns and clubs, and broke in. Fortunately, the family had moved to the city earlier, and only the clothes in the house were looted. When leaving, they destroyed all the furniture in the hall. Furthermore, over ten bandits came to the home of Zhang Weihuang in Jijiazhuang, northwest township, at midnight on the 2nd and broke in, looting all the clothes, ornaments, and silver in the house, resulting in incalculable losses. Furthermore, Yuan Changtai, a resident of the southern township of Juequ City, a small landowner, was suddenly approached by thirty-four bandits at 12:00 p.m. on March 25th. They broke down the door and entered, carrying guns and knives. They first tied up the servants and forced Yuan to hand over silver dollars. After Yuan pleaded repeatedly, he was robbed of fifty-one silver dollars and clothing and jewelry worth approximately four to five hundred gold coins.

Before leaving, they destroyed all the furniture.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Yulong Township: In Xinqiao Township, Yulong Township, Zhenjiang, a resident named Jiang Xuanqing has recently been working as a porter at the Runchang store in Shanghai. He has four daughters and one son, who is sixteen years old. He had just returned home from Shanghai to learn the abacus, planning to learn business at the Baoheng Qianzhuang in Xichang Street, Zhenjiang. Unexpectedly, at 11:00 p.m. last night, six bandits suddenly broke into the house and demanded money from Jiang's wife. Jiang's wife offered the forty yuan she had at home. The bandits were not satisfied and continued to search. They saw Jiang's son lying on the bed and kidnapped him. Jiaxing

Execution of Mutinous Soldiers Who Shot the Battalion Commander: Battalion Commander Huang of the Second Battalion of the Third Regiment of the Security Team stationed in Jiaxing was shot and killed by eleven guard soldiers, including Hu Jiliang, on the night of February 1 when he returned with salary money and stayed overnight at the garrison outside Shanqing Gate, north of the city. They also robbed over 1,000 yuan in salary money and fled with their weapons. The local officials in He reported this and requested a warrant for their arrest. The mutinous soldiers Hu Jiliang, Dai Feiyun, Xu Yongxiang, and Gong Dekang have been captured by the Security Team and escorted to the Security Office for interrogation. They confessed that they were the masterminds behind the shooting of Battalion Commander Huang. Therefore, in accordance with the military law of the army, navy, and air force, the four mutinous soldiers were sentenced to death. On the morning of the 9th, they were escorted from Hangzhou to He and tied up at Xujia坟 outside the North Gate for execution by shooting.

Buddhist Layman Zhu Shaozhang Passes Away: Zhu Shaozhang of Wangdian devoted himself to Buddhism, and his precepts were strict. He often traveled to famous mountains in various places, seeking out Buddhist sites. In recent years, his spiritual power was profound, and he could cure diseases with sincerity. Last year, he came to Shanghai, and the number of people seeking treatment was overwhelming. Zhu only treated those he considered to have karma, and the effects were often miraculous. Now he has returned to his hometown to rest and chants Amitabha Buddha every day, without ceasing for forty days. At 7:00 a.m. on the fourth day of this month, he passed away without illness. By 7:00 p.m., his body was cold everywhere, but the top of his head and hairline still had warm air rising. Those who heard this found it strange.

Scheduled Lottery for Pest Elimination Bonds: The Jiaxing County Pest Elimination Bonds were scheduled to hold a lottery for principal repayment on March 15. However, because the Pest Control Association has been reorganized by the county government, the lottery date has not yet been held. It is now scheduled to hold the eighth repayment lottery in the auditorium of the county government on April 16, and representatives from various agencies are invited to attend the event to supervise.

After receiving the telegram, the regiment commander bound the criminal and executed him at the execution ground today.

Fire in Tu Town: A fire suddenly broke out in Fang Yuansheng Pharmacy on West Street in Tu Town, Linhai Township, at 6:00 a.m. the day before yesterday. The fire was so bright that it lit up the sky and could not be extinguished. It took an hour to extinguish. It is estimated that more than ten houses were destroyed, resulting in losses of approximately 10,000 yuan.

Shenbao Educational News

Special Issue of the National Games · Issue 10

The Ninth Day of the National Games

Football Championship ········ Shanghai Wins

Yesterday, defeated Nanjing 10-1

Baseball Championship ········ Hong Kong Wins

Yesterday, defeated Tianjin 4-2

Swimming Competition ········ Hong Kong, Liaoning, Guangdong Wins

Women's Tennis Singles Finals, Shanghai and Tianjin Each Win One Group

Today's Finals ········ Final Striving

Competition Ends, Closing Ceremony of the Games

Overview of the Venue

Yesterday was the ninth day of the Games, also the eighth day of the competition.

In the morning of the eighth, it was raining heavily, and water accumulated in the competition venues, preventing the start of the games. The competition department announced the postponement of the games for one day, and all scheduled competitions were postponed by one day. Yesterday morning there was drizzle, and the weather cleared up in the afternoon, so the competitions were held one after another.

The men's and women's tennis matches scheduled for the morning were held in the rain. Today, over 20,000 people from various schools and groups in the province and city visited. Tens of thousands of guests also purchased tickets to visit. Among the various ball games, the football and baseball championships have been decided, and the volleyball and tennis matches are in the semi-finals, so the strong are facing strong opponents and their spirits are doubled. The stands were filled early, and there was no space to stand around. The scene was unprecedented. Yesterday's semi-finals are over, and today's competitions are all finals. If there is no heavy rain, they can be concluded in one day. The Games are now scheduled to hold the closing ceremony on the 11th and award prizes the next day. Therefore, today's finals are the day for all the winners to win the final championship. The competition situation should be even more spectacular.

Shanghai Men's Basketball Team

Five People Expelled Yesterday

The Shanghai basketball team almost failed yesterday in the fight for the finals against the Hong Kong team. Fortunately, they made a final effort and won the victory. Several players who have been fighting for days,

Should have been substituted for each other to rest. However, in yesterday's crucial moments, players such as Tan Da　, Wei Haiqing, Kong Guangyi, Chen Wenkui, and Xia Zeren were not all on the court. Those who were on the court were unusually panicked, and their performance declined. The head coach Jiang Xiangqing, general manager Chen Yuze, and coach Xu Zhendong jointly sent letters to Tan and the other five, expelling them from the team and giving them transportation expenses to return to Shanghai.

Yesterday's Results

Football

Shanghai Wins National Football Championship

Yesterday, a Decisive 10-1 Victory Over Nanjing

Nanjing Scores First, Team Fails to Connect

Since both teams entered the National Football Championship, in the preliminary rounds, the second rounds, and the semi-finals, they have been invincible, achieving victory after victory. Yesterday, starting at 2:00 PM, the two teams met in the football field, each deploying their most elite lineups. The Shanghai players, possessing both intelligence and courage, relied on their forward line’s swift passing and their impregnable defense. Their running was fast, and their kicking even faster, resulting in their victory and the championship. The Nanjing players were consistent and indomitable throughout. Although they lost the battle, it was due to their inferior strength, not a failure to fight. It is hoped that the Nanjing team will strive for future success. Victory and defeat are common in military affairs.

The Soccer Skills of the Two Teams

The Shanghai team’s forwards were all physically strong and exceptionally courageous. The team’s strength lies in its ability to work together as a whole, exerting full effort, without selfishness, and with good communication between players. Their passing, heading, dribbling, intercepting, and shooting all have unique qualities. The Nanjing team’s biggest flaw was its lack of cohesion, its inability to put up effective resistance. Individual players focused solely on dribbling, neglecting teamwork and passing. The entire team frequently relied on long passes, rarely engaging in close combat. This was likely due to the excessive pressure from the Shanghai team. However, they charged forward without fear, which was the team’s greatest strength. With long-term training, they could become a formidable force.

Individual Techniques

Sun Enjing, Shanghai’s center-back, guarded and intercepted the enemy, causing them to retreat in awe. He was as steady as a rock, ensuring no mistakes, truly the pillar of the team. Dai Linjing, the center-forward, was brave, agile, and skilled in turning, using his head and feet, passing, and receiving.

The two inside forwards, Chen Xiantian and Chen Jiaqiu, had extraordinary footwork with miraculous variations. They were also able to assess the situation, understand the environment, and exploit the enemy’s weaknesses. Their feints and pushes contained artistic flair.

The wingers were quick and agile, running swiftly, but unfortunately lacked the ability to adapt. The defenders, Li Ning and Chen Pu, were like iron gates at the back. As the saying goes, “It is easier to move a mountain than to move Yue Fei’s army.” Others, like Zhuang Shihong, also performed their duties commendably, without flaws.

In short, Shanghai’s brilliance lies in the similarity of each player. The above comments are based solely on yesterday’s performance. As for the Nanjing team, goalkeeper Tan Zhongzhang repeatedly saved difficult shots, making a significant contribution. His defensive methods were good, using a five-man defensive formation that prevented Shanghai from scoring for the first thirty minutes of the game, which was no easy feat. Others, like Gu Yuanliang and Zhong Guanming, had grasped the basics of dribbling but lacked the ability to adapt.

Commemorative Photo

Five minutes before the game started, the two teams entered the field in an orderly fashion. Photographers and newspaper reporters at the center of the field asked the Shanghai team to pose for a commemorative photo.

Gathering of Heroes After the game began, the Shanghai team immediately launched an offensive. The forwards rushed forward enthusiastically. Dai Linjing, Chen Yutian, and Chen Jiaqiu were like unleashed horses, running and colliding, fighting desperately. Unfortunately, the Nanjing team’s defense was strong, and they were unable to score.

A Bolt from the Blue

Before the Shanghai team could score, the ball was intercepted by the Nanjing team. With a long pass, left-winger Liu Zukan dribbled straight up to an ideal position and shot fiercely at the goal. The ball hit the left post and bounced in. Zhou Xianyan had no way to stop it and could only watch it enter the net. The Nanjing team took the lead.

The Young are Formidable

After conceding a goal, the Shanghai team pressed forward relentlessly. The Nanjing team’s goal was under constant threat. Dai Linjing and Xi Qiaosheng both took fierce shots. Fortunately, goalkeeper Tan Zhongzhang handled the situation appropriately, his hard work was commendable, and he can be considered a rising star.

Returning the Favor

Thirty minutes later, Xi Qiaosheng had a shooting opportunity in the goal area, but his movement was too slow and was blocked by the Nanjing defense. However, the ball was recovered by Zhuang Shihong, who passed it to Chen Jiaqiu, who passed it to Dai. Dai shot fiercely at the goal and scored.

Penalty Kick

At this time, a Nanjing defender suddenly committed a foul in the goal area. The referee awarded a penalty. Dai Linjing kicked the ball in. The Nanjing team fell behind by one goal.

Adding Two More

After scoring two goals, the Shanghai team’s momentum increased. They surrounded the Nanjing team’s goal like an iron barrel. Eventually, Dai Linjing and Xi Qiaosheng scored two more goals in succession.

More Penalty Kicks

Near the end of the first half, Dai Linjing dribbled forward when a Nanjing defender came out to block him. Dai seized the opportunity to lob the ball, which touched the defender’s hand. Another penalty was awarded. Chen Jiaqiu took the kick but missed. Soon after, a Nanjing defender touched the ball again with his hand. Another penalty was awarded, and this time it went in. The first half ended with a score of 5-1, with Shanghai leading.

Charleston Dance

The second half began, and for the first five minutes, nothing was achieved. Suddenly, Dai Linjing got the ball and passed it to Tong Rongwen. Tong dribbled in a winding path, rushed past the defenders, and kicked the ball in. As he charged forward, his body swayed from side to side, resembling a Charleston dance. The posture was quite beautiful.

Diving to Catch the Ball

In the chaos, Wen Chenmao lost his footing. The Nanjing team’s forwards swarmed forward, leaving the Shanghai goal unguarded. At this critical moment, Zhou Xianyan acted with intelligence and dived to catch the ball, saving the game from the brink of defeat. The audience cheered wildly.

Four Goals in a Row

After Fu Heyi scored the seventh goal, the Shanghai team played casually, but their momentum did not diminish. Chen Pu got the ball in the middle of the field and passed it far to the right. Xi Qiaosheng reached it, kicked it in. Soon after, Xi Qiaosheng got the ball, dribbled past the defenders, and passed it to the center. Dai Linjing, waiting by the goal, headed the ball in effortlessly. Finally, Chen Pu got the ball thirty yards from the goal and kicked it in from afar. The ball hit the crossbar and bounced back. Chen Jiaqiu and Fu Heyi followed up closely and kicked it in. Then, the referee blew the whistle to end the game. Shanghai won the championship with a score of 10-1.

Final Expectations

The Far Eastern Games will soon be held in Japan. The team will likely be based on the Shanghai team. It is hoped that the Shanghai team will practice hard in the coming month, travel to the East and win the championship, bringing honor to the country and preserving the reputation of our country’s football for many years. The reporter has high hopes.

Tianjin Shanghai Baseball Game

Photo by Lin Zeren of the Photographic Society

Soccer Scoreboard

Baseball

Hong Kong Wins Championship

Yesterday, a 4-2 Victory Over Tianjin Decides the Hong Kong-Tianjin Baseball Final. The final match between the dragon and tiger teams of Hong Kong and Tianjin took place at 2:00 PM yesterday, with both sides displaying impressive plays. Hong Kong scored first, but Tianjin took the lead with a score of 2-1. In the eighth inning, Hong Kong made a major comeback, winning with a score of 4-2 and securing the baseball championship. Congratulations to the athletes of Hong Kong! Your efforts have not been in vain. The umpires were Zhang Guoxun, Wu Bangwei, and Ma Xun. The scorer was Li Saijun.

Double Play Saves the Day

Hong Kong was the first to bat. The Tianjin pitcher showed off his curved and powerful pitches. Three Hong Kong players were quickly forced out. Tianjin then took their turn. First, Bao Wenpei struck out after three pitches. Second, Zhang Jinglian advanced to first base, followed by Lin Rongbin.

His hit was short and was fielded by the pitcher, who threw to second base. Zhang reached the base first, and then it was thrown to first base. Lin Rongbin was also out. Fortunately, Hong Kong executed a double play, averting a crisis.

A Single Earns a Run

Hong Kong’s Chen Lunying took advantage of an error by the opposing first baseman, occupying first base. Soon after, he stole second base. Chen Yutian aided him by hitting a ground ball to the right, allowing Chen Lunying to run past third base and return to home base. Hong Kong scored first, and Chen Yutian occupied third base. Unfortunately, Chen Yutian was tagged out while attempting to steal home, reducing Hong Kong’s chances of advancing.

A Stalemate Forms

At the start of the third inning, both sides were calm and focused, with tight formations. Occasionally, a player would reach first or second base, but ultimately, they were forced out before they could achieve their goals. There were no changes in the score this inning.

Tianjin Gains the Advantage

In the fourth inning, Tianjin’s Hu Zhensheng hit a single and reached first base. The Hong Kong pitcher lost control, throwing four balls three times. Tianjin was able to load the bases. Hu scored thanks to Luo Qinglong’s single, and Gu Degang’s score was due to the opposing pitcher’s four balls. Tianjin took the lead with a score of 2-1.

Hong Kong Faces Another Threat

The Tianjin pitcher performed exceptionally well. The Hong Kong batters could barely advance. At the same time, the Hong Kong pitcher did not perform his duties well. In this fifth inning,

he threw four balls three times again, sending the runners to first base. All bases were loaded. The situation was serious, and the atmosphere was tense. Fortunately, Hong Kong was able to handle the crisis and turn the danger into safety.

Key to Victory

The sixth inning passed uneventfully, without much change. In the seventh inning, Hong Kong’s Chen Lunying and Chen Qiongren each hit a single. The batters filled up the first three bases. Hong Kong had a great opportunity for a comeback, but unfortunately, it was all for naught. A good opportunity

vanished like smoke.

Hong Kong Suddenly Makes a Comeback

In the seventh inning, Hong Kong’s pitcher Zheng Qiongren and second baseman Chen Lunying switched positions, which was quite effective. Neither team scored in this inning. In the eighth inning, Hong Kong suddenly made a comeback. Liang Zhuoquan hit a single. Immediately, there were runners on each base. Three runners scored, reversing the situation. In the ninth inning, Tianjin tried hard to counterattack, but without success. Hong Kong won the championship with a score of 4-2.

Men's Basketball

Results of Yesterday's Semi-Finals

Shanghai and Tianjin Qualify for Finals

Tianjin Defeats Beiping…46 to 33

The Tianjin Team Wins Consecutive Victories, Unstoppable

Yesterday at 1:00 PM, the Tianjin and Beiping men's basketball teams played their semi-final match. Since the start of the tournament, the Tianjin team had won many games and were sailing smoothly. In terms of strength, they are indeed impressive. The Beiping team had also been the leader of North China. The meeting of these two formidable opponents promised a fierce contest. The spectators crowded around the court, and the Tianjin and Beiping cheerleaders came out to support their teams, their cheers echoing throughout the arena. The details of the two teams' competition are described below.

First to Score

At the sound of the whistle, the two teams began to engage, both using their five-man defensive skills. After about a minute of stalemate, Tianjin's right forward, Tang Baokun, scored a long-range shot, opening the scoring amidst applause. Shortly after, center Liu Jianchang scored again, making it 4-0 to Tianjin. Seeing the strength of their opponents,

the Beiping team quickly called a timeout to regroup. However, after the game resumed, Tianjin still dominated. Their five-man team worked together like a vigorous dragon, showing their true abilities. Although the Beiping team was not weak, their teamwork was not as effective, and their shots were inaccurate, showing signs of panic. The score went from 4-0 to 10-3. Beiping tried hard to counterattack, but to no avail. The score at halftime was 23-14 to Tianjin.

Second Effort

After the break, the game resumed, with Tianjin's Li Qingan replacing right forward Tang Baokun. At this time, the Beiping players fought desperately, with center Wang Yuqing and inside defender Zhao Jiuxuan scoring two consecutive goals, creating great momentum. Tianjin called a timeout.

Yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM, the Shanghai team and Hong Kong team played after the Tianjin and Beiping match. At this point, Shanghai switched to a defensive strategy, and the Hong Kong team attacked with all their might, creating four or five scoring opportunities under the basket. However, they were unlucky. The ball either went outside the basket or bounced off the rim, failing to score. Otherwise, Shanghai would have been defeated. In the last few seconds, Hong Kong finally scored a goal, making the final score 47-45 to Shanghai. The game ended at the same time.

The score in the second half was 28-17, and the Shanghai team won. They will play the Tianjin team today to compete for the championship. Judging from the Shanghai team's performance yesterday, their teamwork and shooting accuracy seemed slightly weaker than the Tianjin team. Without special effort, there is little hope.

Hong Kong 17 points

Guangdong 2 points

The previous day's rain caused the swimming semi-finals to be postponed to yesterday. Although it rained in the morning, it cleared up after lunch, so the event proceeded smoothly according to schedule.

The spectators were still extremely crowded. Liaoning, with high hopes, had male and female cheerleading squads come to cheer and encourage, in high spirits. The four sides of the pool, as well as the trees on the mountain,

were all packed with people, making for a grand spectacle.

Athletes Not Afraid of the Cold

Yesterday, due to the rain, the pool water was rather cold. Initially, when the number of people on the mountain was still sparse, it felt quite calm. As a result, upon seeing the pool water, there seemed to be a sense of reluctance. However, after several test swims, spirits were immediately lifted, and there was no fear of the cold whatsoever.

The athletes were indeed not afraid of the cold.

Liaoning Cheerleading Squad

Liaoning's Shi Xinglong made a name for himself by winning the one-mile race and showing great promise in the 440-yard race (and indeed, he won). Therefore, the Liaoning delegation specially formed male and female cheerleading squads, holding small flags with the characters "Liaoning" stitched on them, half black and half white, showing considerable ingenuity. The female cheerleaders wore neat uniforms, each with a foreign-style red-edged blue-trimmed woven rope garment, all in the same color, which looked very beautiful.

Beautiful to Watch in the Water

Among the swimming events was a diving competition. Originally scheduled as a preliminary round, it was changed to a final due to the small number of participants. This time, scores were not counted, only prizes were awarded. There were six participants in total, four from Hong Kong and two from Liaoning. They first attempted four specified diving styles, then four self-selected styles. Among them, Guo Fengzhen's various diving styles received the most applause and praise from the audience. Some walked into the water, others somersaulted continuously, each style different, some even bizarre. The male and female audience could not stop laughing.

Odds and Ends

Crowded City: Yesterday, in addition to the track and field events, all the other venues held finals, which were exceptionally exciting. All elementary schools in Hangzhou were given a holiday to visit and watch the events, and the city was filled with people. The venues were packed, with deafening cheers. The final battles were of great importance, which is why the whole city was in an uproar.

Sense of Then and Now: The track and field venue was crowded with people the day before yesterday, which was very lively. Yesterday, because there were no competitions, the venue was deserted and silent, almost empty. Those who passed by the venue were filled with a sense of then and now.

Washing Feet in the Clear Stream: Miss Sun Guiyun, who came to the fore this time, has become the focus of attention from all sides. Miss Sun was very tired from the consecutive days of events, so yesterday she went to the lake with her friend Miss Wang Yuan and others to visit famous scenic spots such as Jiang Zhuang, Liu Zhuang, and Three Pools Mirroring the Moon. She encountered rain at Liu Zhuang and accidentally fell into the water. Could it be that because she is good at running and loves the cleanliness of the lake water, she wanted to wash away the dirt accumulated from running around at the venues for days?

Holding Flowers and Smiling: Shi Xinglong from Dalian, who won first place in the 240-yard swimming event, lingered behind after the swimming events were over and the audience had dispersed.

At that moment, the reporter from this newspaper came face to face with him and saw that he was holding a bouquet of fresh flowers and smiling happily, as if he couldn't contain his joy. One can imagine how sweet his heart was.

Triple Strike: Yesterday at 2 PM, during the men's basketball semi-final between Shanghai and Hong Kong, several female students from a certain school in Hangzhou were intently watching from the east side of the court. Unexpectedly, one of the balls from the Hong Kong team

fell on the head of one of the female students, causing a great uproar in the entire venue. Within minutes, two more balls fell in the same area, causing the female students to blush and quickly move away.

Tenfold Profit: Since the opening of the Games, more than 3,000 athletes from all over the country have come to Hangzhou. Although the organizing committee provided dormitories for the athletes to stay, due to the limited number of rooms and poor food, most of them chose to stay in hotels. Therefore, the large and small hotels around West Lake have been booming, making tenfold profits. However, outsiders often say that people from Hangzhou are good at ripping off others. At this time, the hotel owners, in order to make a profit, had to overcharge these outsiders.

Luck and Misfortune: Yesterday afternoon, the final football match between Nanjing and Shanghai was played, and the venue was filled with spectators as never before. Initially, the Shanghai team's performance was poor, but later they turned the tide, and the Nanjing team conceded two penalty kicks. However, during the first penalty kick, the goalkeeper of the Nanjing team slipped and fell, making no effect. During the second penalty kick, the goalkeeper slipped and fell face down, holding onto the ball with both hands. The same penalty kick, but there was luck and misfortune.

Heavily Surrounded: Within the venue, the Shanghai National Goods Machinery Factory Joint Association distributed the magazine "Machinery Association Journal," which was compiled and printed by the association, every day at the venue. The magazine's text was simple and interesting, and it was especially popular among elementary school students. Each time it was distributed, the person holding the magazine would be surrounded, unable to move forward or backward. Moreover, most of them were lively children, so it was impossible to refuse them with harsh words. Therefore, they were in a dilemma, unable to move forward.

Philippine Man's Prediction of Far Eastern Games Titles Translated by Qian Yiqin

Japan Will Win: Track and Field, Swimming, Tennis Titles

Philippines Will Win: Basketball, Volleyball Titles

China Will Win: Soccer Title

All-Around Ball is Key to the Title

People of Our Country, Urgently Need to Strive

This article was written by Dr. Regino R. Ylanan, a well-known executive of the Philippine Athletic Association, originally titled "Our Chances in The Olympi" and published in the third issue of the Philippine "Sports Weekly" this year. His views are unique. Taking advantage of the gathering of athletes from all over the country during the National Games in Hangzhou, I urgently translated it to serve as a stone from another mountain. When our athletes read it, they should consider how to work hard and encourage themselves.

Since the Far Eastern Games began until 1921, the host country has always won the Games title. For example, the Games in Manila in 1913 were won by the Philippines, the Games in Shanghai in 1915 were won by China, and the Games in Osaka in 1917 were won by Japan. These are all clear evidence. However, after the Games in Shanghai in 1921 and 1927 were won by the Philippines and Japan respectively, this sequence changed.

If we want to know the Philippines' chances in the next Games, there are several important factors that need to be studied in detail. Let's break them down: (1) Japan's rapid progress in various sports; (2) the prolongation of the Chinese civil war; (3) India's participation in the Far Eastern Games. Let's first talk about the first point. Japan has made great progress in track and field and swimming in recent years. Its performance in the World Summer Beak Games held in Amsterdam, Holland, and the performances held in Tokyo and Manchuria last year are amazing. To be fair, Japan is the only country that can compete with the strong United States in swimming at the next Summer Olympics. The same is true for tennis. Its players have defeated the world's best players. Therefore, Japan's strength in the Davis Cup will be even better than in the past.

Now let's talk about the second point. Whenever the Games are held in another country, China has never had a full delegation attend. Now that the civil war is in full swing, it may not be possible to send many representatives to participate. China's strength lies in national sports, especially in soccer, basketball, and volleyball. In the previous Games, China had no position in track and field and swimming. Judging from the current results, China may not be able to share Japan's points in the next Games. The only sport in which it always wins is soccer. As for basketball and volleyball, it will inevitably compete with the Philippines as hard as possible.

Now let's discuss the third point. India's participation in the Games will cause considerable changes in the Games title. If India does send representatives to Tokyo this year, the number will not be large. This can be asserted. From an economic point of view alone, there is no difference in the cost of sending athletes to Japan and to the Philippines. However, if India does send a full delegation to attend, it will be harmful to China and Japan, but beneficial to the Philippines. This is because India is quite strong in soccer and may be able to seize China's authority and replace it. Its tennis players also have a reputation in the international arena. There are also many long-distance runners, and they often take away Japan's long-distance points in the Summer Olympics.

The decision of the Far Eastern Games overall title is based on the number of first places won in the events. The scoring method is a 5-3-1 system.

If there is a tie, the team with the highest score wins. According to the results of the previous Games and the performance of Chinese, Japanese, and Philippine athletes last season, Japan will win track and field, tennis, and swimming in the next Games, China will win soccer, and the Philippines will win basketball and volleyball. Baseball and all-around sports will be the final key to determining who wins the Games title.
